gdp_var = {
	value = root.gdp
	min = 1
}
capital_gdp_var = {
	value = capital.gdp
	min = 1
}
capital_gdp_ratio = {
	value = capital_gdp_var
	divide = gdp_var
}

GDP_dif_1_final = {
	value = var:GDP_dif_1
}
GDP_dif_5_final = {
	value = var:GDP_dif_5
}
GDP_dif_10_final = {
	value = var:GDP_dif_10
}

highest_gdp = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_global_highest_gdp =yes
		}
		add = gdp
	}
}
ratio_with_highest_gdp = {
	value = GDP
	divide = highest_gdp
}

loyalist_fraction_pop = {
	value = loyalist_fraction
}
radical_fraction_pop = {
	value = radical_fraction
}
var_global_country_ranking = {
	value = country_rank
}
national_capacity_reference_currency = {
	value = 1
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = global_monetary_reference
		}
		add = national_capacity
	}
}

ratio_with_national_capacity_reference_currency = {
	value = national_capacity
	divide = national_capacity_reference_currency
}

army_size_var = {
	value = 0
	add = army_size
}
navy_size_var = {
	value = 0
	add = navy_size
}

currency_quantity_sell = {
	value = 0.5
	if = {
		limit = {
			or  = {
				#has_modifier = extreme_weak_currency voir si on change
				var:currency_crisis = 1
				var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 1
				scope:overrated_currency_country_owner.infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
			}
		}
		add = 0.5
	}
}

	}
}

bg_bank_lvl = {
	value = 0
	every_scope_building = {
		limit = {
			is_building_group = bg_bank
		}
		add = level
	}
}
bg_bank_lvl_by_base_rate = {
	value = bg_bank_lvl
	multiply = {
		value = {
		 	add = 10
		 	subtract = base_rate_percentage_decimal
		}
		divide = 9
	}
	max = bg_bank_lvl
	min = 1
	round = yes
}

	multiply = private_bank_borrowings_year_var_2

num_states_var = {
	add = root.num_states
}
import_export_disable = {
	value = 0
	if = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				has_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
				has_modifier = extreme_weak_currency
			}
		}
		add = 1
	}
}

enemy_capital_is_occuped = {
	value = 0
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			is_at_war = yes
			has_war_with = ROOT
		}
		capital = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					controller = ROOT
					has_modifier = central_bank_place
				}
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}
enemy_stats_is_occuped = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			is_at_war = yes
			has_war_with = ROOT
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					controller = ROOT
				}
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

institution_economic_central_bank_lvl = {
	value = 0
	if = {
		limit = {
			institution_investment_level = {
				institution = institution_economic_central_bank
				value >= 1
			}

		}
		add = 0.5
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			institution_investment_level = {
				institution = institution_economic_central_bank
				value >= 2
			}

		}
		add = 0.5
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			institution_investment_level = {
				institution = institution_economic_central_bank
				value >= 3
			}

		}
		add = 0.5
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			institution_investment_level = {
				institution = institution_economic_central_bank
				value >= 4
			}

		}
		add = 0.5
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			institution_investment_level = {
				institution = institution_economic_central_bank
				value >= 5
			}

		}
		add = 0.5
	}
}

#manufacture_stock limit
manufacture_stock_product_by_pcs = {
	value = 0
	every_scope_building = {
		limit = {
			is_building_type = building_ef_private_construction
		}
		add = modifier:goods_output_manufacture_stock_add
		#multiply = overbuilding_regulation_factor_revers
	}
}
manufacture_stock_product_by_pcs_real = {
	value = manufacture_stock_product_by_pcs
	multiply = var:overbuilding_regulation_factor_revers_fix
}
manufacture_stock_product_by_pcs_rate = {
	value = manufacture_stock_product_by_pcs_real
	divide = manufacture_stock_market_goods_sell_orders #mon 100%
}
overbuilding_regulation_factor = {
    value = 0
    if = {
        limit = {
            manufacture_stock_product_by_pcs_rate > 0.10
            manufacture_stock_product_by_pcs_rate < 0.40
        }
        # Régulation progressive de 0 à 70 entre 10% et 40%
        add = manufacture_stock_product_by_pcs_rate
        subtract = 0.10
        divide = 0.30
        multiply = 70
    }

    # En dessous ou égal à 10%, add = 0
}
overbuilding_regulation_factor_revers = {
	value = 100
	subtract = overbuilding_regulation_factor
	#multiply = -1
	divide = 100
	# subtract = 0.15
	# min = -1
}

extreme_weak_currency_solution_count_sc = {
    value = 0
    add = var:extreme_weak_currency_solution_count_player
    add = var:extreme_weak_currency_solution_count
}

	}

difference_with_average_gold_exchange_rate_currencies = {
	value = money_value_in_gold #money_value_rapported_inflation
	divide = global_var:money_value_median
}
difference_with_average_gold_exchange_rate_currencies_revers = {
	value = 1
	subtract = difference_with_average_gold_exchange_rate_currencies
	multiply = -1
}
difference_with_average_gold_exchange_rate_currencies_revers_normalized = {
	value = difference_with_average_gold_exchange_rate_currencies_revers
	multiply = -1
}
difference_with_average_gold_exchange_rate_currencies_revers_100 = {
	value = difference_with_average_gold_exchange_rate_currencies_revers_normalized
	multiply = 100
}

player_has_central_bank = {
	value = 0
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			is_player = yes
			has_modifier = has_central_bank
		}
		add = 1
	}
}
money_value_of_player = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			is_player = yes
		}
		value = money_value
	}
}
money_value_rapported_inflation_of_player = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			is_player = yes
		}
		value = money_value_rapported_inflation
	}
}
money_supply_of_player = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			is_player = yes
		}
		value = money_supply
	}
}
money_supply_stockpile_by_other_country_of_player = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			is_player = yes
		}
		value = money_supply_stockpile_by_other_country
	}
}

#devaluation
devaluation_rate_normalized = {
	value = var:devaluation_rate
	add = 100
	divide = 100
}
money_value_predicted_devaluation = {
	value = national_capacity
	divide = money_supply_predicted_devaluation
	max = 100
}
money_supply_predicted_revaluation = {
	value = money_supply
	add = money_supply_predicted_add_revaluation_1
}
money_supply_predicted_devaluation = {
	value = money_supply
	multiply = devaluation_rate_normalized
}
money_supply_predicted_add_devaluation_1 = {
	value = money_supply_predicted_devaluation
	subtract = money_supply
}
inflation_value_predicted_devaluation = {
	add = devaluation_rate_normalized
	subtract = 1
	divide = var:devaluation_time #pas besoin de le validé car les bouton sont intouchable
}
devaluation_time_month = {
	value = var:devaluation_time
	multiply = 12
}
devaluation_time_1_month = { #special for exchange control
	value = var:devaluation_time_1
	multiply = 12
}
devaluation_time_week = {
	value = var:devaluation_time
	multiply = 52
}
inflation_value_predicted_devaluation_month = {
	value = var:devaluation_rate
    divide = devaluation_time_month
}
money_supply_to_add_per_month = { #valeur à ajouter par an
	value = 0
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:devaluation_on = 1
		}
		add = var:money_supply_predicted_add_devaluation_1_month_valided #valided to save the vare
		divide = devaluation_time_month
	}
}
devaluation_on_time_scripted = {
	value = 0
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:devaluation_on = 1
		}
		add = devaluation_time_month
		subtract = var:devaluation_on_time
	}
}

#revaluation
revaluation_rate_normalized = {
	value = 100
	subtract = var:revaluation_rate
	divide = 100
}

	value = national_capacity
	divide = money_supply_predicted_revaluation
	max = 100
}

	value = money_supply
	add = money_supply_predicted_add_revaluation_1
}

	value = money_supply_state #money_supply
	multiply = revaluation_rate_normalized
}

	value = money_supply_state_predicted_revaluation #money_supply
	subtract = money_supply_state
}

	add = revaluation_rate_normalized
	subtract = 1
	multiply = var:revaluation_time
}

	value = var:revaluation_time
	multiply = 12
}

	value = var:revaluation_time_1
	multiply = 12
}

	value = var:revaluation_time
	multiply = 52
}

	value = var:revaluation_rate
    divide = revaluation_time_month
	multiply = -1

		divide = revaluation_time_month
	}

# ███╗   ███╗ ██████╗ ███╗   ██╗███████╗██╗   ██╗    ██╗   ██╗ █████╗ ██╗     ██╗   ██╗███████╗

# ╚═╝     ╚═╝ ╚═════╝ ╚═╝  ╚═══╝╚══════╝   ╚═╝╚══════╝ ╚═══╝  ╚═╝  ╚═╝╚══════╝ ╚═════╝ ╚══════╝

money_value = {

	if = {
		limit = {
			not = {
				has_modifier = has_central_bank
			}
		}
		value = money_value_no_bc
	}

	#has_central_bank subjectt/no market owner
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = has_central_bank
		}
		value = money_value_0
	}

	#subjectt
	if = {
		limit = {
	        market_owner_is_root_4 = no
        }
		if = {
			limit = {
				market.owner = {
					has_modifier = has_central_bank
				}
			}
			value = market.owner.money_value_0

			#subject
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_subject_custom_trigger = yes
					market.owner = {
						is_player = no
					}
				}
				multiply = subject_overlord_gdp_ratio_revers
				#min = 0.01
			}

			#no market.owner
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_subject_custom_trigger = no
					market.owner = {
						is_player = no
					}
				}
			    value = market.owner.money_value_0
			}

			#market.owner = player
			if = {
				limit = {
					market.owner = {
						is_player = yes
					}
				}
				divide = market.owner.var:parity_scaled_by_the_overlord
				add = 1
				min = 0.01
			}
		}
	}

	# #no market owner
	# if = {
	# 	limit = {
	# 		market_owner_is_root_4 = no
	# 		is_subject = no
	# 	}
	# 	if = {
	# 		limit = {
	# 			market.owner = {
	# 				has_modifier = has_central_bank
	# 			}
	# 		}
	# 		value = market.owner.money_value_0
	# 	}
	# }

	#max = revaluation_money_value_max
	max = 100
	min = 0.0001
}
money_value_target_2_in_gold = {
	min = 0.0001

	if = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_standard
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_exchange_standard
			}
		}
		add = var:money_value_target_2
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_silver_standard
		}
		value = var:money_value_target_2
		multiply = silver_to_gold_rate
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_bimetallism_standard
		}
		value = var:money_value_target_2
		#multiply = bimetallic_rate_silver_to_gold
	}
}
money_value_0 = {
	value = 0

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_fiat_standard
			#has_law = law_type:law_no_monetary_system
		}
		value = 0.01
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_silver_standard
				has_law = law_type:law_bimetallism_standard
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_standard
			}
		}
		value = national_capacity
		divide = money_supply
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_gold_exchange_standard
		}
		add = money_value_by_reference_currency
	}

	#max = 10
}
money_value_in_gold = {
	value = 0
	if = {
		limit = {
			market_owner_is_root_4 = yes
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_standard
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_exchange_standard
			}
		}
		add = money_value
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			market_owner_is_root_4  = yes
			has_law = law_type:law_silver_standard
		}
		add = money_value_silver_standard_in_gold
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			market_owner_is_root_4  = yes
			has_law = law_type:law_bimetallism_standard
		}
		add = money_value_bimetallism_standard_in_gold
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			or  = {
			    market_owner_is_root_4 = no
			    is_subject = yes
		    }
		}
		add = money_value
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type_2
	}

	min = 0.0001
}
money_value_no_bc = {
	value = 0.01
}

	multiply = gold_to_silver_rate

money_value_prevision_new_currency_in_gold = {
	value = global_var:money_value_median

		}

		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_silver_standard

	}

		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_bimetallism_standard
		}
		value = money_value_target_real
		#multiply = bimetallic_rate_silver_to_gold #bimetallic_rate
	}
}

national_capacity_in_gold = {
	min = 0.0001

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_gold_standard
			#no law_gold_exchange_standard
		}
		add = national_capacity
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_silver_standard
		}
		add = central_bank_reserves_silver_standard_in_gold
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_bimetallism_standard
		}
		add = central_bank_reserves_bimetallism_standard_in_gold
	}
}

test_bourse  = {
	value = owner.var:circulating_dollar_united_states_dollar_c_var_1
	add = var:stockpiling_dollar_united_states_dollar_state_1
	multiply = owner.var:money_value_target_1
	multiply = 1 #0.9
}


national_capacity = {
	value = 1
	if = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_silver_standard
				has_law = law_type:law_bimetallism_standard
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_standard
			}
		}
		add = central_bank_reserves #en fonction du type de metal
		add = gold_loaned_to_central_bank_in_national_metal # en or pour gold standart et bimetalisme et convertis en equivalent argent pour le silver
		add = var:trade_balance_in_gold_fixe # en or ou en metal sion utilise le money_value_in_gold
	}


	#tu dois armoniser le bimetalisme pour que la majoritait des 2 sources:
	# 	- add = gold_loaned_to_central_bank_in_national_metal # en or pour gold standart et bimetalisme et convertis en equivalent argent pour le silver
	# 	- add = var:trade_balance_in_gold_fixe # en or ou en metal sion utilise le money_value_in_gold
	# doivent etre en or, c'est uniquement dans le silver standart que c'est valeur sont adpaté pour avoir un esquivalent argent
	#concernant la reserve dans le bimetalisme l'or est compté à 1 et le silver est calculer dans sont équivalent or ce qui veux dire que c'est comme un gold standart quand la reserve est principalement composé d'or mais comme un silver standart dépendent du prix international du silver quand elle est composé de silver principalement


	min = 0.01
}

national_capacity_ratio = {
	add = national_capacity
	divide = money_supply
}
central_bank_reserves_ratio = {
	add = central_bank_reserves
	divide = national_capacity
}
gold_loaned_to_central_bank_ratio = {
	add = gold_loaned_to_central_bank_in_national_metal
	divide = national_capacity
}
trade_balance_in_gold_ratio = {
	add = var:trade_balance_in_gold_fixe
	divide = national_capacity
}

gold_loaned_to_central_bank_in_national_metal = {
	value = 0
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_gold_standard
			#no law_gold_exchange_standard
		}
		add = var:gold_loaned_to_central_bank_fix
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_silver_standard
		}
		add = var:gold_loaned_to_central_bank_fix
		multiply = gold_to_silver_rate
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_bimetallism_standard
		}
		add = var:gold_loaned_to_central_bank_fix
		#multiply = bimetallic_rate_gold_to_silver
	}
}

gold_loaned_to_central_bank_in_national_metal_silver = {
	value = var:gold_loaned_to_central_bank_fix
	multiply = gold_to_silver_rate
}

gold_loaned_to_central_bank_in_national_metal_bimetalic = {
	value = var:gold_loaned_to_central_bank_fix 
}

gold_loaned_to_central_bank_in_national_metal_gold = {
	value = var:gold_loaned_to_central_bank_fix
}

############################################################################################################################################################
#central_bank_reserves
############################################################################################################################################################

central_bank_reserves = {
	value = 0.01
	add = central_bank_metal_reserves_state
}

central_bank_metal_reserves_state = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_standard
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_exchange_standard
			}
		}
		add = gold_state_native_for_stockpile
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_silver_standard
		}
		add = silver_state_native_for_stockpile
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_bimetallism_standard
		}
		add = bimetallic_state_native_for_stockpile
	}
}

central_bank_metal_reserves_state_per_month = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_standard
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_exchange_standard
			}
		}
		add = stockpiling_central_bank_metal_reserves_gold_standard
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_silver_standard
		}
		add = stockpiling_central_bank_metal_reserves_silver_standard
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_bimetallism_standard
		}
		#add = stockpiling_central_bank_metal_reserves_bimetallism_standard
		add = stockpiling_central_bank_metal_reserves_bimetallism_standard_in_gold
	}
}

gold_state_native_for_stockpile = {
	value = 0
	add = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
				}
				add = var:gold_state_1
			}
		}
	}
}
silver_state_native_for_stockpile = {
	value = 0
	add = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
				}
				add = var:silver_state_1
			}
		}
	}
}
bimetallic_state_native_for_stockpile = {
	value = 0
	add = gold_state_native_for_stockpile
	add  = {
		add = silver_state_native_for_stockpile
		divide = gold_to_silver_rate
	}
}

silver_state_native_for_stockpile_in_gold = {
	value = 0
	add  = {
		add = silver_state_native_for_stockpile
		divide = gold_to_silver_rate
	}
}

trade_balance_gold_to_silver_rate = {
    add = var:trade_balance_in_gold_fixe
    multiply = gold_to_silver_rate
}
trade_balance_bimetallic_rate_gold_to_silver = {
    add = var:trade_balance_in_gold_fixe
    multiply = bimetallic_rate_gold_to_silver
}
trade_balance_bimetallic_rate_silver_to_gold = {
    add = var:trade_balance_in_gold_fixe
	divide = gold_to_silver_rate
	multiply = bimetallic_rate_gold_to_silver #normal tkt c'est inversé car le calcule e la trade balance concidére que c'est de l'or que l'on scale à de la argent -> dont on fait l'invese pour avoir la bonne quantité
}

import_value_in_gold_previsionel = {
	value = debt_in_national_currency #=debt_in_national_currency_in_gold à multiplié par la money value future


		multiply = {
			add = var:money_value_target_1
			#multiply = bimetallic_rate_silver_to_gold
		} #= money_value_target_real_in_gold
}

trade_balance_fiat_to_silver = {
	value = {
		value = excess_foreign_state_currency_in_gold_no_excess_in_gold_sc
		add = excess_in_gold_sc
   		multiply = gold_to_silver_rate
	}
	subtract = import_value_in_gold
}
trade_balance_fiat_to_bimetallic = {
	value = {
		add = excess_foreign_state_currency_in_gold_no_excess_in_gold_sc
		#multiply = bimetallic_rate_gold_to_silver
		add = excess_in_gold_sc
	}
	subtract = import_value_in_gold
}
trade_balance_fiat_to_gold = {
	value = {
		value = excess_foreign_state_currency_in_gold_no_excess_in_gold_sc
		add = excess_in_gold_sc
	}
	subtract = import_value_in_gold
}

trade_balance_silver_to_gold = {
	value = {
		value = excess_foreign_state_currency_in_gold_no_excess_in_gold_sc #excess_foreign_state_currency_in_gold
		multiply = silver_to_gold_rate
		add = excess_in_gold_sc
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_player = yes
		}
		subtract = {
			value = debt_in_national_currency
			multiply = {
				add = var:money_value_target_1
				multiply = silver_to_gold_rate
			} #= money_value_target_real_in_gold
		}
	}
}
trade_balance_silver_to_bimetallic = {
	value = {
		value = excess_foreign_state_currency_in_gold_no_excess_in_gold_sc #excess_foreign_state_currency_in_gold
		multiply = silver_to_gold_rate
		add = excess_in_gold_sc
	} 
	subtract = {
		value = debt_in_national_currency
		multiply = {
			add = var:money_value_target_1
			multiply = silver_to_gold_rate
		} #= money_value_target_real_in_gold
	} 
}

trade_balance_bimetallic_to_gold = {
	value = {
		value = excess_foreign_state_currency_in_gold_no_excess_in_gold_sc
 		add = excess_in_gold_sc
	}
	subtract = {
		value = debt_in_national_currency
		multiply = var:money_value_target_1
	}
}

	value = {
		value = excess_foreign_state_currency_in_gold_no_excess_in_gold_sc
		multiply = gold_to_silver_rate
		add = excess_in_gold_sc
	}
	subtract = {
		value = debt_in_national_currency
		multiply = {
			add = var:money_value_target_1
			multiply = gold_to_silver_rate
		} #= money_value_target_real_in_gold
	}
}

##############
#monetary_systeme_silver_standard
##############
central_bank_metal_reserves_state_silver_standard = {
	value = silver_state_native_for_stockpile
}
central_bank_reserves_silver_standard = {
	value = central_bank_metal_reserves_state_silver_standard
	add = gold_loaned_to_central_bank_in_national_metal_silver

	#trade balance
	if = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				var:law_fiat_standard = 1 
				var:law_no_monetary_system = 1    
			}
		}
		add = trade_balance_fiat_to_silver
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:law_silver_standard = 1  
		}
		add = var:trade_balance_in_gold_fixe
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:law_bimetallism_standard = 1 
		}
		add = trade_balance_bimetallic_to_silver #idem trade_balance_gold_to_silver
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				var:law_gold_standard = 1 
				var:law_gold_exchange_standard = 1   
			}
		}
		add = trade_balance_gold_to_silver #idem trade_balance_bimetallic_to_silver
	}
}
central_bank_reserves_silver_standard_in_gold = {
	value = central_bank_metal_reserves_state_silver_standard
	add = gold_loaned_to_central_bank_in_national_metal_silver
	add = var:trade_balance_in_gold_fixe
	multiply = silver_to_gold_rate
}
money_value_silver_standard = {
	value = central_bank_reserves_silver_standard
	divide = money_supply
}
money_value_silver_standard_in_gold = {
	value = money_value_silver_standard
	multiply = silver_to_gold_rate
}
money_value_silver_standard_in_gold_50 = {
	value = money_value_silver_standard_in_gold
	multiply = 0.50
}
money_value_silver_standard_in_gold_33 = {
	value = money_value_silver_standard_in_gold
	multiply = 0.66
}
stockpiling_central_bank_metal_reserves_silver_standard = {
	value = 0
	#add = var:stockpiling_silver_var_2

	add = silver_market_goods_sell_orders

	#multiply = 1000
	multiply = 100

	multiply = 4 #month


	multiply = gold_to_silver_rate
}
stockpiling_central_bank_metal_reserves_silver_standard_native = {
	value = 0
	#add = var:stockpiling_silver_var_2

	add = silver_market_goods_sell_orders

	#multiply = 1000

	multiply = 4 #month
}
stockpiling_central_bank_metal_reserves_silver_standard_in_gold= {
	value = stockpiling_central_bank_metal_reserves_silver_standard

	multiply = silver_to_gold_rate
}
##############
#monetary_systeme_bimetallism_standard
##############
central_bank_metal_reserves_state_bimetallism_standard = {
	value = bimetallic_state_native_for_stockpile
}

#serie de variable par type de standart qui prenne toute la veurl 1 quand la loi est set 
#lorsqu'ne autre loi est set on utilise cetta variable pour savoir ou on était 
#puis on rest tout et on met 1 sur la nouvelle loi 

central_bank_reserves_bimetallism_standard = {
	value = central_bank_metal_reserves_state_bimetallism_standard #ok
	add = gold_loaned_to_central_bank_in_national_metal_bimetalic #ok

	#trade balance
	if = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				var:law_no_monetary_system = 1 
				var:law_fiat_standard = 1 
				# has_law = law_type:law_fiat_standard
				# has_law = law_type:law_no_monetary_system
			}
		}
		add = trade_balance_fiat_to_bimetallic
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			#has_law = law_type:law_silver_standard 
			var:law_silver_standard = 1 
		}
		add = trade_balance_silver_to_bimetallic
	} 
	if = {
		limit = {
			# has_law = law_type:law_bimetallism_standard
			var:law_bimetallism_standard = 1 
		}
		add = var:trade_balance_in_gold_fixe
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				# has_law = law_type:law_gold_standard
				# has_law = law_type:law_gold_exchange_standard
				var:law_gold_standard = 1 
				var:law_gold_exchange_standard = 1 
			}
		}
		add = var:trade_balance_in_gold_fixe #trade_balance_gold_to_bimetallic
	}
}
central_bank_reserves_bimetallism_standard_in_gold = {
	value = central_bank_reserves_bimetallism_standard
	add = gold_loaned_to_central_bank_in_national_metal_bimetalic
	add = var:trade_balance_in_gold_fixe
	#multiply = bimetallic_rate_silver_to_gold
}
money_value_bimetallism_standard = { #valeur utiliser pour definir la money valu tareget et qui change car on change de loi avant de faire le calcule
	value = central_bank_reserves_bimetallism_standard
	divide = money_supply
}
money_value_bimetallism_standard_in_gold = {
	#value = money_value_bimetallism_standard #pb avec le fiatt stta	andar affiche 0 ddonc je l'ai remis sinnon just money_value
	#multiply = bimetallic_rate_silver_to_gold

	add  = {
		add = money_value_silver_standard_in_gold
		multiply = weight_silver
	}
	add  = {
		add = money_value_gold_standard
		multiply = weight_gold
	}
}
bimetallism_standard_proportional_silver= {
	value = money_value_silver_standard_in_gold
	multiply = weight_silver
}

bimetallism_standard_proportional_gold = {
	value = money_value_gold_standard
	multiply = weight_gold
}

	value = money_value_bimetallism_standard_in_gold #pb avec le fiatt stta	andar affiche 0 ddonc je l'ai remis sinnon just money_value
	multiply = 0.50
}
money_value_bimetallism_standard_in_gold_33 = {
	value = money_value_bimetallism_standard_in_gold #pb avec le fiatt stta	andar affiche 0 ddonc je l'ai remis sinnon just money_value
	multiply = 0.66
}

		add = silver_market_goods_sell_orders

		multiply = 100
		multiply = 4 #month
		multiply = gold_to_silver_rate

		multiply = 100
		multiply = 4 #month
		#multiply = gold_to_silver_rate
	}
}

	add = stockpiling_central_bank_metal_reserves_silver_standard_in_gold

}

#monetary_systeme_gold_standard

central_bank_metal_reserves_state_gold_standard = {
	value = gold_state_native_for_stockpile
}
central_bank_reserves_gold_standard = {
	value = central_bank_metal_reserves_state_gold_standard
	add = gold_loaned_to_central_bank_in_national_metal_gold

	#trade balance
	if = {
		limit = {
			or = { 
				var:law_no_monetary_system = 1 
				var:law_fiat_standard = 1 
			}
		}
		add = trade_balance_fiat_to_gold
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:law_silver_standard = 1  
		}
		add = trade_balance_silver_to_gold
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:law_bimetallism_standard = 1 
		}
		add = var:trade_balance_in_gold_fixe	
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				var:law_gold_standard = 1 
				var:law_gold_exchange_standard = 1  
			}
		}
		add = var:trade_balance_in_gold_fixe
	}
}

	value = central_bank_reserves_gold_standard
	divide = money_supply

# rarity_factor = {
# 	value = 1
# 	divide = {
# 		value = building_ef_private_construction_lvl
# 		multiply = 0.35   # a = 0.35
# 		divide = 50       # b = 50
# 		add = 1
# 	}
# }
rarity_factor = {
    value = 1
    divide = {
        value = building_ef_private_construction_lvl
        # pente "a" conditionnelle inline
        multiply = {
            value = 0.35
            if = {          # quand beaucoup de bâtiments, on adoucit
                limit = { building_ef_private_construction_lvl >= 150 }
                value = 0.30
            }
        }
        divide = 50
        add = 1
    }
}

valid_purchasable_currency_amount = {
	if = {
		limit  = {
			purchasable_currency_amount > valid_purchasable_currency_amount_10
		}
		add = valid_purchasable_currency_amount_10
	}
	if = {
		limit  = {
			purchasable_currency_amount < valid_purchasable_currency_amount_10
			purchasable_currency_amount > valid_purchasable_currency_amount_9
		}
		add = valid_purchasable_currency_amount_9
	}
	if = {
		limit  = {
			purchasable_currency_amount < valid_purchasable_currency_amount_9
			purchasable_currency_amount > valid_purchasable_currency_amount_8
		}
		add = valid_purchasable_currency_amount_8
	}
	if = {
		limit  = {
			purchasable_currency_amount < valid_purchasable_currency_amount_8
			purchasable_currency_amount > valid_purchasable_currency_amount_7
		}
		add = valid_purchasable_currency_amount_7
	}
	if = {
		limit  = {
			purchasable_currency_amount < valid_purchasable_currency_amount_7
			purchasable_currency_amount > valid_purchasable_currency_amount_6
		}
		add = valid_purchasable_currency_amount_6
	}
	if = {
		limit  = {
			purchasable_currency_amount < valid_purchasable_currency_amount_6
			purchasable_currency_amount > valid_purchasable_currency_amount_5
		}
		add = valid_purchasable_currency_amount_5
	}
	if = {
		limit  = {
			purchasable_currency_amount < valid_purchasable_currency_amount_5
			purchasable_currency_amount > valid_purchasable_currency_amount_4
		}
		add = valid_purchasable_currency_amount_4
	}
	if = {
		limit  = {
			purchasable_currency_amount < valid_purchasable_currency_amount_4
			purchasable_currency_amount > valid_purchasable_currency_amount_3
		}
		add = valid_purchasable_currency_amount_3
	}
	if = {
		limit  = {
			purchasable_currency_amount < valid_purchasable_currency_amount_3
			purchasable_currency_amount > valid_purchasable_currency_amount_2
		}
		add = valid_purchasable_currency_amount_2
	}
	if = {
		limit  = {
			purchasable_currency_amount < valid_purchasable_currency_amount_2
			purchasable_currency_amount > valid_purchasable_currency_amount_1
		}
		add = valid_purchasable_currency_amount_1
	}
}

valid_purchasable_currency_amount_1 = {
	value = 0
}

income_150 = {
	value = income
	multiply = 1.5
}

	value = income
	multiply = 1.75
}

	value = income

	value = income
	multiply = 2.25

	value = income
	multiply = 2.5
}
authorized_debt_interest = {
 	value = 0
	if = {
		limit = {
			expenses < income_150
		}
		add = 0.25
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			expenses > income_150
			expenses < income_175
		}
		add = 0.20
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			expenses > income_175
			expenses < income_200
		}
		add = 0.15
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			expenses > income_200
			expenses < income_225
		}
		add = 0.10
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			expenses > income_225
			expenses < income_250
		}
		add = 0.05
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			expenses > income_250
		}
		add = 0
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			country_credit > 0
		}
		add = -1
	}
	min = 0
}

gold_market_goods_sell_orders = {
	if  = {
		limit = {
			not = {
				or = {
					is_subject_custom_trigger = yes
					market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = yes
					no_indepeendeent_market = yes
				}
			}
		}
		value = {
			add = owner.market.mg:gold.market_goods_sell_orders
		}
	}
}
silver_market_goods_sell_orders = {
	if  = {
		limit = {
			not = {
				or = {
					is_subject_custom_trigger = yes
					market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = yes
					no_indepeendeent_market = yes
				}
			}
		}
		value = {
			add = owner.market.mg:silver.market_goods_sell_orders
		}
	}
}

	# }
	# min = 0

}
bimetallic_rate_gold_to_silver = {
	#value = var:bimetallic_rate_gold_to_silver_determined
	#divide = bimetallic_rate_silver_to_gold

	if = {
		limit  = {
			has_law = law_type:law_bimetallic_ratio_no
		}
		add = gold_to_silver_rate
	}
	if = {
		limit  = {
			has_law = law_type:law_bimetallic_ratio_10
		}
		add = 10
	}
	if = {
		limit  = {
			has_law = law_type:law_bimetallic_ratio_15
		}
		add = 15
	}
	if = {
		limit  = {
			has_law = law_type:law_bimetallic_ratio_20
		}
		add = 20
	}
}

	}

		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_silver_standard
		}

		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_bimetallism_standard
		}
		add = 1 #bimetallic_rate_gold_to_silver
	}
	min = 0.0001
}

	value = gold_to_silver_rate
	subtract = bimetallic_rate_gold_to_silver
	divide = gold_to_silver_rate

	min = 0
	max = 0.15   # 15% max de drain/an
}

	value = gold_state_native_for_stockpile
	multiply = misalignment_rate_gold_drain
}

	multiply = gold_to_silver_rate
}

	subtract = gold_to_silver_rate
	divide = bimetallic_rate_gold_to_silver

	min = 0
	max = 0.15   # 15% max de drain/an

inflation_value_for_currency = {
	value = 100
	if = {
		limit = {
			inflation_value_100 > 0
		}
		subtract = inflation_value_100
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			inflation_value_100 < 0
		}
		subtract = inflation_value_100
	}
	divide = 100
}
inflation_value_100 = {
	value = inflation_value
	multiply = 100
}
inflation_value = {
	value = 0
	add = var:inflation_on_consumer_goods_rolling_inflation_6_months
	add = var:inflation_on_energy_rolling_inflation_6_months
	add = var:inflation_on_raw_material_rolling_inflation_6_months
	add = var:inflation_on_manufactured_goods_rolling_inflation_6_months
	add = var:inflation_on_military_equipment_rolling_inflation_6_months
	add = money_value_dif_01_rolling_inflation_6_months_limited
	add = monetary_policy_inflation
}

money_value_dif_01_rolling_inflation_6_months_limited = {
	add = var:money_value_dif_01_rolling_inflation_6_months

	# if = {
	# 	limit = {
	# 		not = {
	# 			has_modifier = foreign_exchange_controls
	# 		}
	# 	}
	# 	max = 0.1
	# 	min = -0.1
	# }

	max = 0.1
	min = -0.1
}

inflation_value_for_modifier = {
	value = inflation_value
	max = 1
	min = -1
}

	if = {
		limit = {
			inflation_on_consumer_goods_market_value < 0
		}
		subtract = inflation_on_consumer_goods_market_value
	}
}

	value = 0

		limit = {
			devaluation_money_value_target_trigger = yes
		}
		add = 1
	}
}

revaluation_money_value_target_trigger_var = {
	value = 0
	if  = {
		limit = {
			revaluation_money_value_target_trigger = yes
		}
		add = 1
	}
}

devaluation_money_value_target = {
	value = 0
	if = {
		#1
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 1.1
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}
	if = {
		#1.1
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1.1
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 1.2
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 1
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}
	if = {
		#1.2
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1.2
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 1.3
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 1.1
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}
	if = {
		#1.3
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1.3
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 1.4
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 1.2
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}
	if = {
		#1.4
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1.4
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 1.5
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 1.3
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}
	if = {
		#1.5
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1.5
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 1.6
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 1.4
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}
	if = {
		#1.6
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1.6
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 1.7
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 1.5
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}
	if = {
		#1.7
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1.7
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 1.8
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 1.6
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}
	if = {
		#1.8
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1.8
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 1.9
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 1.7
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}
	if = {
		#1.9 si au dessu alors à chaque dévaluation il fait perdre 10%
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1.9
		}
		value = {
			add = var:money_value_target_1
			multiply = 0.9
		}
		#multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}

	# if = {
	# 	#compren pas
	# 	limit = {
	# 		var:money_value_target_1 > revaluation_money_value_max
	# 	}
	# 	value = revaluation_money_value_max
	# }
}
revaluation_money_value_target = {
	value = 0

	if = { #réévalue à la valeur de la moyenne si la cible est a 0
		limit = {
			var:money_value_target_1 = 0
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio <  1
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 0.9
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}

	if = {
		#0.8
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 0.9
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 1
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}
	if = {
		#0.8
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 0.8
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 0.9
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}
	if = {
		#0.7
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 0.7
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 0.8
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}
	if = {
		#0.6
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 0.6
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 0.7
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}
	if = {
		#0.5
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 0.5
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 0.6
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}
	if = {
		#0.4
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 0.4
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 0.5
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}
	if = {
		#0.3
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 0.3
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 0.4
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}
	if = {
		#0.2
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 0.2
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 0.3
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}

	max = revaluation_money_value_max
}
overlord_money_value_target = {
	value = overlord.var:money_value_target_1
}

devaluation_money_value_target_in_gold = {
	value = 0
	if = {
		#1
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 1.1
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}
	if = {
		#1.1
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1.1
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 1.2
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 1
	}
	if = {
		#1.2
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1.2
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 1.3
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 1.1
	}
	if = {
		#1.3
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1.3
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 1.4
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 1.2
	}
	if = {
		#1.4
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1.4
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 1.5
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 1.3
	}
	if = {
		#1.5
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1.5
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 1.6
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 1.4
	}
	if = {
		#1.6
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1.6
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 1.7
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 1.5
	}
	if = {
		#1.7
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1.7
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 1.8
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 1.6
	}
	if = {
		#1.8
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1.8
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 1.9
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 1.7
	}
	if = {
		#1.9
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 1.9
		}
		value  = {
			add = var:money_value_target_1
			multiply = 0.9
		}
	}

	if = {
		#
		limit = {
			var:money_value_target_1 > revaluation_money_value_max
		}
		value = revaluation_money_value_max
		divide = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}
}
revaluation_money_value_target_in_gold = {
	value = 0

	if = { #réévalue à la valeur de la moyenne si la cible est a 0
		limit = {
			var:money_value_target_1 = 0
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio <  1
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio > 0.9
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
	}

	if = {
		#0.8
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 0.9
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 1
	}
	if = {
		#0.8
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 0.8
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 0.9
	}
	if = {
		#0.7
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 0.7
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 0.8
	}
	if = {
		#0.6
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 0.6
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 0.7
	}
	if = {
		#0.5
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 0.5
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 0.6
	}
	if = {
		#0.4
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 0.4
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 0.5
	}
	if = {
		#0.3
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 0.3
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 0.4
		multiply = rate_by_law_metal_type
	}
	if = {
		#0.2
		limit = {
			money_value_median_and_money_value_in_gold_ratio < 0.2
		}
		value = global_var:money_value_median
		multiply = 0.3
	}

	#max = revaluation_money_value_max
}

pool_growth_rate_thanks_to_borrowing = {
	value = 0
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		}
		add = 0.10
		multiply = private_bank_borrowings_year_var_2
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		}
		add = 0.09
		multiply = private_bank_borrowings_year_var_2
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		}
		add = 0.08
		multiply = private_bank_borrowings_year_var_2
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		}
		add = 0.07
		multiply = private_bank_borrowings_year_var_2
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		}
		add = 0.06
		multiply = private_bank_borrowings_year_var_2
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		}
		add = 0.05
		multiply = private_bank_borrowings_year_var_2
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		}
		add = 0.04
		multiply = private_bank_borrowings_year_var_2
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		}
		add = 0.03
		multiply = private_bank_borrowings_year_var_2
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		}
		add = 0.02
		multiply = private_bank_borrowings_year_var_2
	}
}

#gui
pool_growth_rate_thanks_credit_score = {
	value = 0
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		}
		add = 0.10
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		}
		add = 0.09
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		}
		add = 0.08
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		}
		add = 0.07
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		}
		add = 0.06
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		}
		add = 0.05
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		}
		add = 0.04
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		}
		add = 0.03
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		}
		add = 0.02
	}
}
private_bank_borrowings_year = {
	value = private_bank_funds
	multiply = pool_growth_rate_thanks_to_borrowing

	if = {
		limit = {
			private_bank_funds_pourcent < 0.05
		}
		add = var:direct_transfer
	}
}

#gui
private_bank_borrowings_year_var_1 = {
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage > 0.01
		}
		value = var:base_rate_percentage
		multiply = 10
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage < 0.01
		}
		value = var:base_rate_percentage #0.95
		multiply = 2
	}
}
base_rate_percentage_revers = {
	value = 1
	subtract = {
		value = var:base_rate_percentage
		multiply = 10

	}
}

base_rate_percentage_decimal = {
	value = var:base_rate_percentage
	multiply = 100
}

private_bank_borrowings_year_var_2 = {
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage > 0.01
		}
		value = base_rate_percentage_revers
	}

	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.01
		}
		value = 1
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.0095
		}
		value = 2
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.0090
		}
		value = 3
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.0085
		}
		value = 4
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.0080
		}
		value = 5
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.0075
		}
		value = 6
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.0070
		}
		value = 7
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.0065
		}
		value = 8
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.0060
		}
		value = 9
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.0055
		}
		value = 10
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.0050
		}
		value = 11
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.0045
		}
		value = 12
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.0040
		}
		value = 13
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.0035
		}
		value = 14
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.0030
		}
		value = 15
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.0025
		}
		value = 16
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.0020
		}
		value = 17
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.0015
		}
		value = 18
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.0010
		}
		value = 19
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:base_rate_percentage = 0.0005
		}
		value = 20
	}
}

	}

		limit  = {
			law_dinar_monetary_system_SS_trigger = yes

#private bank

total_privat_bank = {
	every_in_list = {
		variable = privat_bank_variable_list_ordered
		add  = 1
	}
}

total_bank_funds = {
	value = private_bank_funds
	add = funds_from_foreign_debt_total
}

private_bank_funds_per_private_bank = {
	value = private_bank_funds
	divide = total_privat_bank
}

private_bank_funds_per_private_bank_add_foreign_debt = {
	value = owner.private_bank_funds_per_private_bank
	add = funds_from_foreign_debt #1000000 #les fond issu de la dette étrangère
}
